TITLE      Charged particle emission in reactions of 15-MeV       10827001    9 
            neutrons with isotopes of chromium, iron, nickel, and 10827001   10 
            copper.                                               10827001   11 
INC-SOURCE (D-T) 400-keV deuterons on rotating titanium tritide   10827001   12 
            target                                                10827001   13 
SAMPLE     2.5-cm diameter foil with diaphragm to avoid           10827001   14 
            contaminants from foil holders.                       10827001   15 
METHOD     Triple lens magnetic quadrupole spectrometer used.     10827001   16 
            Different reaction angles obtained by moving transport10827001   17 
            system along its axis. Nine different current settings10827001   18 
            used for magnets to cover energy range of emitted     10827001   19 
            particles                                             10827001   20 
DETECTOR   (MAGSP) Triple lens magnetic quadrupole spectrometer   10827001   21 
           (SIBAR) Pair of silicon surface barrier detectors, 15  10827001   22 
            and 1500 micro-meters thick, spaced 19-mm apart.      10827001   23 
CORRECTION Energy spectra corrected for energy loss in target foil10827001   24 
ERR-ANALYS (ERR-1,,3.) polyethylene stopping power (<3%),         10827001   25 
           (ERR-2) solid angle of target to neutron source ratio  10827001   26 
             for CH2 or CD2 compared to that of sample foils (8%),10827001   27 
           (ERR-3) target foil thickness errors (2.5%)            10827001   28 
             Other sources are described in Subents.              10827001   29 
             Combined errors were 11-15% for protons, 15-20% for  10827001   30 
             alpha particles, and 20-30% for deuterons.           10827001   31
